				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Jesus nahm zu sich die Zwölfe, BWV 22 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>5 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1723 in Leipzig/Köthen
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Jesus nahm zu sich die Zwölfe
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Jesus took the twelve under Him
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Translations
</th>
<td><span title="ja">イエス十二弟子を召寄せて</span>; <span title="he">Jesus nahm zu sich die Zwölfe, רי"ב 22</span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Authorities
</th>

<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Johann_Sebastian" title="Category:Bach, Johann Sebastian">Bach, Johann Sebastian</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>BWV 22&#160;; BC A 48
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IJB 345
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Key
</th>
<td>G minor
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>5 movements:
<ol><li> Arioso and Chorus (tenor, bass): Jesus nahm zu sich die Zwölfe und sprach (G&#160;minor)
</li><li> Aria (alto): Mein Jesu, ziehe mich nach dir (C&#160;minor)
</li><li> Recitativo (bass): Mein Jezu, ziehe mich, so werd ich laufen (E<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;major-B&#160;major)
</li><li> Aria (tenor): Mein alles in allem, mein ewiges Gut (B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;major)
</li><li> Chorale: Ertöt uns durch dein Güte (B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;major)
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>
